# LoCoBench-Agent Task

## Task Information

## Task Title

Architectural Analysis for Decoupling the Authentication Service

## Description

IntraLedger BlogSuite is a complex, monolithic C++ web application. Its user authentication system has proven to be robust and secure. As part of a new company-wide initiative, management wants to extract this authentication logic into a standalone, centralized Single Sign-On (SSO) service that can be used by other internal applications. Before development begins, a thorough architectural analysis is required to understand the full scope and impact of this refactoring. The codebase is highly modularized, but the module names (`module_XX.cpp`) are non-descriptive, requiring deep code analysis to understand their purpose and inter-dependencies.

## Your Task

Your task is to act as a principal software architect and analyze the IntraLedger BlogSuite codebase to prepare for the authentication service extraction. You must produce a report that addresses the following points:

1.  **Core Component Identification:** Identify the primary C++ source file(s) that constitute the core of the authentication and session management system. Justify your choices by describing the key functions or classes within these files (e.g., password hashing, user registration, session token generation).

2.  **Dependency Mapping:** Identify all other modules within the `src/` directory that are directly coupled to the core authentication/session components. For each dependent module you identify, provide the filename and a brief explanation of the dependency's nature (e.g., 'module_23.cpp depends on the auth system to verify user permissions before processing a request').

3.  **Decoupling Strategy:** Propose a high-level architectural strategy to decouple the authentication logic from the main application. Your strategy should define a clear boundary or contract (e.g., an abstract interface, a set of API endpoints) that would allow the BlogSuite to communicate with a future external authentication service with minimal changes to the dependent modules.

## Expected Approach

An expert developer would not rely on simple keyword searches like 'auth' or 'login', especially given the obfuscated filenames. The process would be systematic:

1.  **Start at the Entry Point:** The developer would first try to identify the main request handling loop or router, likely by examining `test_main.cpp` for clues on how the system is initialized or by searching for common web server patterns (e.g., handling HTTP requests) across the files.

2.  **Trace a User-Centric Feature:** They would trace the execution path of a feature that requires authentication, such as creating a new blog post or viewing a user profile. This involves following function calls and data flow across multiple modules.

3.  **Identify Data Structures:** The expert would look for central data structures like `User`, `Session`, or `Credentials` and find where they are defined and manipulated. The module defining these structures is often a core component.

4.  **Analyze Dependencies:** Using the identified core auth module(s) as a starting point, the developer would use static analysis techniques (mentally or with tools) to find all modules that `#include` its headers or call its public functions. They would build a mental dependency graph.

5.  **Propose an Abstraction:** For the decoupling strategy, the expert would recommend introducing an abstraction layer, such as an `IAuthService` interface (a common C++ pattern using an abstract base class). This follows the Dependency Inversion Principle, allowing the core application to depend on the interface, not the concrete implementation, making it easy to swap the local implementation with a remote (SSO) one later.

## Evaluation Criteria

- **Correctness of Core Module Identification:** Did the agent correctly identify `module_12.cpp` and `module_35.cpp` as the primary authentication and session components?
- **Completeness of Dependency Analysis:** How many of the key dependent modules (`23`, `10`, `61`, `7`, `41`) were correctly identified?
- **Accuracy of Dependency Rationale:** Is the agent's explanation for *why* each module is a dependency accurate and specific?
- **Soundness of Decoupling Strategy:** Does the proposed strategy effectively abstract the authentication logic? Is the use of an abstract class/interface or a similar pattern correctly identified as the best practice?
- **Architectural Acumen:** Does the response demonstrate an understanding of high-level software design principles like Dependency Inversion, Separation of Concerns, and API contracts, or does it offer a naive, surface-level solution?

     6→ *  PasswordResetService – Implements the workflow for secure, rate-limited
     7→ *  password-reset requests.  The service is agnostic of the underlying storage
     8→ *  and e-mail delivery mechanisms; it relies purely on small, well-defined
     9→ *  interfaces that are expected to be injected at run-time by the IOC-container

    14→ *  asynchronous e-mail via the Job Processor, and (4) validates tokens on
    15→ *  subsequent password-reset attempts.  Basic in-memory rate-limiting protects

     2→/**
     3→ *  IntraLedger BlogSuite
     4→ *  File: src/module_74.cpp
     5→ *
     6→ *  SecureTokenService
     7→ *  -------------------
     8→ *  Provides generation and validation of signed, short-lived tokens that are
     9→ *  used throughout the authentication middleware (password resets, e-mail
    10→ *  confirmations, OAuth state, etc.).  The implementation is intentionally
    11→ *  kept self-contained to avoid any tight coupling with the rest of the
    12→ *  security stack.  Tokens are similar in spirit to JWTs but use a reduced
    13→ *  header and an application-specific payload to minimize bloat.
    14→ *
    15→ *  Dependencies:
    16→ *      • OpenSSL   – HMAC-SHA256 signing
    17→ *      • nlohmann/json – Lightweight JSON serialization
    18→ *      • spdlog    – Structured logging
    19→ *
    20→ *  The public API is thread-safe, exception-safe, and respects RAII.
    21→ */

109-assistanttext-
I have completed the architectural analysis for decoupling the authentication service from the IntraLedger BlogSuite codebase. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Key Findings

### Core Authentication Modules Identified

1. **module_74.cpp** - `SecureTokenService`: JWT-like token generation and validation using HMAC-SHA256
2. **module_56.cpp** - `PasswordResetService`: Secure password reset workflow with rate limiting
3. **module_33.cpp** - `LoginAttemptThrottler`: Brute force protection with per-user and per-IP tracking
4. **module_39.cpp** - `PermissionEvaluator`: RBAC with permission caching
5. **module_52.cpp** - `PermissionService`: Voter-based access control (similar to Spring Security)
6. **module_46.cpp** - `TokenBucketRateLimiter`: Token bucket rate limiting middleware

### Dependent Modules

- **module_51.cpp**: Email notifications (password reset emails)
- **module_24.cpp**: Search service with RBAC-aware filtering
- **module_64.cpp**: Search service with role-based result filtering
- **module_66.cpp**: Content metrics with user context for deduplication

### Decoupling Strategy

I proposed introducing an `IAuthenticationService` abstract interface following the **Dependency Inversion Principle**. This approach:

1. Wraps existing modules in a `LocalAuthenticationService` implementation
2. Allows future implementation of a `RemoteSSOAdapter` for external SSO integration
3. Enables dependent modules to use the interface via dependency injection
4. Supports configuration-driven swapping between implementations

The complete solution with code evidence, architectural diagrams, and detailed implementation strategy has been written to `/logs/agent/solution.md`.

The implementation is intentionally\n *  kept self-contained to avoid any tight coupling with the rest of the\n *  security stack.  Tokens are similar in spirit to JWTs but use a reduced\n *  header and an application-specific payload to minimize bloat.\n *\n *  Dependencies:\n *      \u2022 OpenSSL   \u2013 HMAC-SHA256 signing\n *      \u2022 nlohmann/json \u2013 Lightweight JSON serialization\n *      \u2022 spdlog    \u2013 Structured logging\n *\n *  The public API is thread-safe, exception-safe, and respects RAII.\n */\n\n#include <openssl/hmac.h>\n#include <openssl/rand.h>\n\n#include <nlohmann/json.hpp>\n#include <spdlog/spdlog.h>\n\n#include <chrono>\n#include <cstddef>\n#include <cstdint>\n#include <exception>\n#include <iomanip>\n#include <optional>\n#include <sstream>\n#include <string>\n#include <string_view>\n#include <vector>\n\nnamespace intraledger::security\n{\nusing Json     = nlohmann::json;\nusing Clock    = std::chrono::system_clock;\nusing Seconds  = std::chrono::seconds;\nusing TimePoint= std::chrono::time_point<Clock>;\n\n/*--------------------------------------------------------\n * Exceptions\n *-------------------------------------------------------*/\nclass TokenError : public std::runtime_error\n{\npublic:\n    using std::runtime_error::runtime_error;\n};\n\nclass TokenExpired : public TokenError\n{\npublic:\n    TokenExpired() : TokenError(\"Token has expired\") {}\n};\n\nclass TokenInvalid : public TokenError\n{\npublic:\n    explicit TokenInvalid(const std::string& msg = \"Invalid token\")\n        : TokenError(msg) {}\n};\n\n/*--------------------------------------------------------\n * Base64URL helpers\n *-------------------------------------------------------*/\nnamespace detail\n{\nconstexpr char kAlphabet[] =\n    \"ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ\"\n    \"abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz\"\n    \"0123456789-_\";\n\ninline std::string base64url_encode(const std::vector<uint8_t>& data)\n{\n    BIO* b64 = BIO_new(BIO_f_base64());\n    BIO_set_flags(b64, BIO_FLAGS_BASE64_NO_NL); static_cast<int>(cfg_.secretKey.size()),\n                         EVP_sha256(), nullptr) != 1)\n        {\n            HMAC_CTX_free(ctx);\n            throw TokenError(\"HMAC_Init_ex failed\");\n cryptographically secure random hex\n     * string of length `byteCount * 2`.\n     *---------------------------------------------------*/\n    static std::string randomHex(std::size_t byteCount)\n    {\n        std::vector<uint8_t> buf(byteCount);\n        if (RAND_bytes(buf.data(), static_cast<int>(buf.size())) != 1)\n            throw TokenError(\"RAND_bytes failed\");\n\n        std::ostringstream oss;\n        oss << std::hex << std::setfill('0');\n        for (uint8_t b : buf)\n            oss << std::setw(2) << static_cast<int>(b);\n        return oss.str();\n    }\n\n    /*----------------------------------------------------\n     * constantTimeEquals\n     *\n     * Compares two byte sequences in constant time to\n     * mitigate timing attacks.\n     *---------------------------------------------------*/\n    static bool constantTimeEquals(std::span<const uint8_t> a,\n                                   std::span<const uint8_t> b)\n    {\n Although the\n *  implementation relies only on the C++17 standard library, it follows the\n *  same coding conventions as the rest of BlogSuite and hooks into the\n *  platform\u2019s diagnostic facilities.\n *\n *  NOTE: All time values are expressed in steady_clock time to avoid issues\n *  with system-clock adjustments (NTP, daylight-savings, leap seconds).\n */\n\n#include <chrono>\n#include <condition_variable>\n#include <cstdint>\n#include <cstdlib>\n#include <exception>\n#include <fmt/core.h>\n#include <functional>\n#include <memory>\n#include <mutex>\n#include <optional>\n#include <shared_mutex>\n#include <string>\n#include <thread>\n#include <unordered_map>\n\n#include \"core/Logger.hpp\"           // Project-wide asynchronous logger\n#include \"core/RuntimeConfig.hpp\"    // Access to strongly-typed env/config\n#include \"util/ScopeGuard.hpp\"       // Simple defer/RAII helpers\n\nnamespace intraledger::security\n{\nusing Clock          = std::chrono::steady_clock;\nusing Duration       = Clock::duration;\nusing TimePoint      = Clock::time_point;\nusing milliseconds   = std::chrono::milliseconds;\nusing seconds        = std::chrono::seconds;\n\n/**\n *  TokenBucket\n *  -----------\n *  POJO holding the refill algorithm state for a single key.\n */\nclass TokenBucket final\n{\npublic:\n    TokenBucket(std::size_t maxTokens, double refillRatePerSec) noexcept\n        : _maxTokens(static_cast<double>(maxTokens))\n        , _refillRatePerSec(refillRatePerSec)\n        , _tokens(_maxTokens)\n        , _lastRefill(Clock::now())\n    {\n    }\n\n    TokenBucket(const TokenBucket&)            = delete;\n    TokenBucket& operator=(const TokenBucket&) = delete;\n    TokenBucket(TokenBucket&&)                 = default;\n    TokenBucket& operator=(TokenBucket&&)      = default;\n\n    /**\n     *  Attempt to remove one token from the bucket. Returns true if a token\n     *  was successfully consumed, false otherwise.\n     */\n    bool consume()\n    {\n        refill();\n\n        if (_tokens >= 1.0)\n        {\n            _tokens -= 1.0;\n            return true;\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     *  Returns how many whole tokens are currently available. Mainly used\n     *  for diagnostics.\n     */\n    std::size_t availableTokens() const noexcept\n    {\n        return static_cast<std::size_t>(_tokens);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     *  Update internal token count based on elapsed time.\n     */\n    void refill()\n    {\n        auto now          = Clock::now();\n        auto elapsed      = std::chrono::duration_cast<milliseconds>(now - _lastRefill);\n        double newTokens  = (elapsed.count() / 1000.0) * _refillRatePerSec;\n\n        if (newTokens > 0.0)\n        {\n            _tokens      = std::min(_maxTokens, _tokens + newTokens);\n            _lastRefill  = now;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     *  Touch the bucket so the cleaner thread won\u2019t prematurely delete it.\n     */\n    void touch() noexcept { _lastAccess = Clock::now(); }\n\n    /**\n     *  Age since last access; used by the cleaner thread for eviction.\n     */\n    Duration age() const noexcept { return Clock::now() - _lastAccess; }\n\nprivate:\n    double     _maxTokens          { 0.0 };\n    double     _refillRatePerSec   { 0.0 };\n    double     _tokens             { 0.0 };\n    TimePoint  _lastRefill         { Clock::now() };\n    TimePoint  _lastAccess         { Clock::now() };\n};\n\n/**\n *  TokenBucketRateLimiter\n *  ----------------------\n *  Thread-safe map of token buckets keyed by an arbitrary string (IP, user\n *  id, session id, etc.).  Buckets are lazily created on first access and\n *  garbage-collected after `bucketTTL` of inactivity by a low-priority\n *  maintenance thread.\n */\nclass TokenBucketRateLimiter final\n{\n    // Reasonable default: 100 buckets, refill 5 tokens/second, bucket size 20\n    static constexpr std::size_t kDefaultCapacity        = 20;\n    static constexpr double      kDefaultRefillPerSecond = 5.0;\n    static constexpr seconds     kDefaultBucketTTL       = seconds{ 300 };      // 5 min\n    static constexpr seconds     kDefaultCleanupInterval = seconds{ 30 };\n\npublic:\n    struct Settings\n    {\n        std::size_t maxTokens         { kDefaultCapacity };\n        double      refillRatePerSec  { kDefaultRefillPerSecond };\n        seconds     bucketTTL         { kDefaultBucketTTL };\n        seconds     cleanupInterval   { kDefaultCleanupInterval };\n    };\n\n    explicit TokenBucketRateLimiter(const Settings& settings = {})\n        : _settings(settings)\n        , _shutdownFlag(false)\n        , _maintenanceThread(&TokenBucketRateLimiter::maintenanceLoop, this)\n    {\n        BLOGSUITE_LOG_INFO(\n            \"TokenBucketRateLimiter started: max={}, refill={}/s, TTL={}s\", \n            _settings.maxTokens, \n            _settings.refillRatePerSec, \n            _settings.bucketTTL.count());\n    }\n\n    ~TokenBucketRateLimiter() noexcept\n    {\n        {\n            std::lock_guard lk(_maintenanceMutex);\n            _shutdownFlag = true;\n            _maintenanceCv.notify_all();\n        }\n        if (_maintenanceThread.joinable())\n            _maintenanceThread.join();\n    }\n\n    TokenBucketRateLimiter(const TokenBucketRateLimiter&)            = delete;\n    TokenBucketRateLimiter& operator=(const TokenBucketRateLimiter&) = delete;\n\n    /**\n     *  Attempts to consume a single token for the provided key.  Returns\n     *  true if the operation is permitted, false otherwise.\n     *\n     *  Thread-safe and lock-free on the common path; uses a shared-mutex to\n     *  handle bucket map mutations.\n     */\n    bool allow(const std::string& key)\n    {\n        auto bucket = getOrCreateBucket(key);\n        if (!bucket)\n            return false;\n\n        bool permitted = bucket->consume();\n        bucket->touch();\n\n        if (!permitted)\n        {\n            BLOGSUITE_LOG_WARN(\"RateLimiter blocked key='{}' (remaining={})\",\n                               key, bucket->availableTokens());\n        }\n        return permitted;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     *  Returns the number of whole tokens available for the given key.\n     *  Mainly used for introspection endpoints so does not optimize for speed.\n     */\n    std::optional<std::size_t> available(const std::string& key)\n    {\n        std::shared_lock rlk(_mapMutex);\n        if (auto it = _buckets.find(key); it != _buckets.end())\n            return it->second.availableTokens();\n        return std::nullopt;\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    /**\n     *  Retrieve (or lazily create) a bucket for the given key.  Uses an\n     *  upgrade path from shared to unique lock to keep contention low.\n     */\n    TokenBucket* getOrCreateBucket(const std::string& key)\n    {\n        // First try with read lock\n        {\n            std::shared_lock rlk(_mapMutex);\n            auto             it = _buckets.find(key);\n            if (it != _buckets.end())\n                return &it->second;\n        }\n        // Upgrade to write lock for insertion\n        {\n            std::unique_lock wlk(_mapMutex);\n            auto             [it, inserted] = _buckets.try_emplace(\n                key, _settings.maxTokens, _settings.refillRatePerSec);\n            return &it->second;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     *  Background thread that periodically removes stale buckets to prevent\n     *  unbounded memory growth.  The thread exits when the object is\n     *  destructed.\n     */\n    void maintenanceLoop()\n    {\n        BLOGSUITE_LOG_DEBUG(\"RateLimiter maintenance thread started\");\n        while (true)\n        {\n            std::unique_lock lk(_maintenanceMutex);\n            _maintenanceCv.wait_for(lk, _settings.cleanupInterval, [this]() { return _shutdownFlag; });\n            if (_shutdownFlag)\n                break;\n\n            const auto now   = Clock::now();\n            const auto ttl   = _settings.bucketTTL;\n\n            std::size_t removed = 0;\n            {\n                std::unique_lock mapLock(_mapMutex);\n                for (auto it = _buckets.begin(); it != _buckets.end();)\n                {\n                    if (it->second.age() >= ttl)\n                    {\n                        it = _buckets.erase(it);\n                        ++removed;\n                    }\n                    else\n                    {\n                        ++it;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n            if (removed > 0)\n            {\n                BLOGSUITE_LOG_DEBUG(\"RateLimiter cleaned {} expired bucket(s)\", removed);\n            }\n        }\n        BLOGSUITE_LOG_DEBUG(\"RateLimiter maintenance thread stopped\");\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    Settings                                       _settings;\n    std::unordered_map<std::string, TokenBucket>   _buckets;\n\n    mutable std::shared_mutex                      _mapMutex;\n\n    // Maintenance thread state\n    std::atomic<bool>                              _shutdownFlag;\n    std::mutex                                     _maintenanceMutex;\n    std::condition_variable                        _maintenanceCv;\n    std::thread                                    _maintenanceThread;\n};\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Global Singleton                                                           */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n *  Provides a process-wide instance of the rate-limiter using runtime config.\n *  Because BlogSuite is a single executable, we keep the global hidden inside\n *  this translation unit to avoid static-init-order issues.\n */\nstatic TokenBucketRateLimiter& globalLoginRateLimiter()\n{\n    static TokenBucketRateLimiter::Settings s {\n        core::RuntimeConfig::get<std::size_t>(\"security.rateLimiter.maxTokens\", 10),\n        core::RuntimeConfig::get<double>(\"security.rateLimiter.refillPerSec\", 2.0),\n        seconds{ core::RuntimeConfig::get<int>(\"security.rateLimiter.bucketTTL\", 300) },\n        seconds{ core::RuntimeConfig::get<int>(\"security.rateLimiter.cleanupInterval\", 60) }\n    };\n\n    static TokenBucketRateLimiter instance { s };\n    return instance;\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Public API                                                                 */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nnamespace api\n{\n\n/**\n *  Checks if a request originating from `clientKey` is allowed to proceed.\n *  Proxy/wrapper that delegates to the TU-local singleton.\n *\n *  Example usage:\n *\n *    if (!api::isLoginAttemptAllowed(ipAddress)) {\n *        return HttpResponse::too_many_requests();\n *    }\n */\nbool isLoginAttemptAllowed(const std::string& clientKey)\n{\n    return globalLoginRateLimiter().allow(clientKey);\n}\n\n/**\n *  Exposes bucket diagnostics to other parts of the system (metrics, admin UI).\n */\nstd::optional<std::size_t> tokensAvailable(const std::string& clientKey)\n{\n    return globalLoginRateLimiter().available(clientKey);\n}\n\n} // namespace api\n} // namespace intraledger::security\n```",

*/\ndouble score_document(std::string_view text,\n                      const std::vector<std::string>& search_terms)\n{\n    if (search_terms.empty())\n        return 0.0;\n\n around the first term hit.\n */\nstd::string make_snippet(std::string_view text,\n                         const std::vector<std::string>& search_terms,\n                         std::size_t context = std::size_t pos = lowercase.find(term);\n        if (pos != std::string_view::npos &&\n            (best_pos == std::string_view::npos || pos < best_pos))\n            best_pos = pos;\n    }\n\n    if sc = ranking::score_document(rec.content, search_terms);\n            std::string snip = ranking::make_snippet(rec.content, search_terms);\n            out.push_back(Result{std::move(rec), sc, std::move(snip)});\n        }\n\n        // Step 4: Sort by score desc, then published_at desc\n        std::ranges::stable_sort(out, [](auto const& a, auto const& b)\n        {\n            if (a.score != b.score)\n                return a.score > b.score;\n            return a.article.published_at > b.article.published_at;\n        });\n\n        spdlog::info(\"Search for '{}' returned {} m_lexer.peek().position };\n                }\n\n                return std::make_unique<QueryNode>(FieldFilter { fieldName, std::move(valueNode) });\n            }\n\n            /* Plain term */\n std::make_unique<QueryNode>(Phrase { phraseTok.lexeme });\n        }\n\n        throw ParseError { \"Unexpected token '\" + m_lexer.peek().lexeme + \"'\", m_lexer.peek().position };\n    }\n\n    //    bool match(TokenType t)\n    {\n        if (peek(t))\n        {\n            m_lexer.consume();\n            return true;\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    void expect(TokenType t)\n    {\n        if (!match(t))\n            throw ParseError { \"Expected different token\", m_lexer.peek().position };\n    }\n\n    bool peek(TokenType t) const { return m_lexer.peek().type == t; }\n\n                   [](unsigned char c) { return static_cast<char>(std::tolower(c)); });\n        return out;\n    }\n\n    static bool is_whitelisted_field(const std::string& field)\n    {\n SqlFragment\n{\n    std::string              sql;     // WHERE clause without the \"WHERE\" keyword\n    std::vector<std::string> params;  // positional parameters to bind in order\n};\n\nclass SqlTranslator\n{\npublic:\n    // Compile AST into SQL WHERE fragment\n    SqlFragment compile(const QueryNode& root)\n    {\n        m_buffer.clear();\n        m_params.clear();\n It follows the classic\n *  \u201cvoter\u201d strategy found in many security frameworks (e.g., Spring Security)\n *  and adds a thread-safe, bounded LRU cache to avoid re-computing expensive\n *  decisions for hot resources.\n *\n *  NOTE:\n *    The surrounding application provides concrete repositories\n *    (UserRepository, ArticleRepository, etc.) via dependency injection.\n *    Those interfaces are forward-declared here to keep translation units\n *    self-contained while remaining link-time compatible with the rest of\n *    the monolith.\n */\n\n#include <algorithm>\n#include <chrono>\n#include <cstddef>\n#include <functional>\n#include <iostream>\n#include <list>\n#include <memory>\n#include <mutex>\n#include <optional>\n#include <shared_mutex>\n#include <stdexcept>\n#include <string>\n#include <unordered_map>\n#include <utility>\n#include <vector>\n\nnamespace intraledger::blogsuite::security {\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Forward declarations for repositories supplied by the main application\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\nclass IUserRepository;\nclass IArticleRepository;\nclass ISubscriptionRepository;\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Common domain definitions\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\nenum class Role {\n    Reader,\n    Author,\n    Editor,\n    Admin,\n    SuperAdmin\n};\n\nstruct UserContext final\n{\n    std::string            id;\n    std::vector<Role>      roles;\n    bool                   authenticated{false};\n\n    bool hasRole(Role r) const noexcept\n    {\n        return std::find(roles.begin(), roles.end(), r) != roles.end();\n    }\n};\n\nstruct ResourceDescriptor final\n{\n    std::string ownerId;\n    bool        isPublic  {true};\n    bool        isPremium {false};\n};\n\n// Convenience hashing for cache key\nstruct PermissionKey final\n{\n    std::string userId;\n    std::string resourceId;\n    std::string action; // e.g. \"read\", \"edit\", \"delete\"\n\n    bool operator==(const PermissionKey& rhs) const noexcept\n    {\n        return userId == rhs.userId &&\n               resourceId == rhs.resourceId &&\n               action == rhs.action;\n    }\n};\n\nstruct PermissionKeyHasher\n{\n    std::size_t operator()(const PermissionKey& k) const noexcept\n    {\n        std::hash<std::string> h;\n        return (h(k.userId) ^ (h(k.resourceId) << 1)) ^ (h(k.action) << 2);\n    }\n};\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// LRU Cache (thread-safe)\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\ntemplate <typename Key, typename Value, typename Hasher = std::hash<Key>>\nclass LRUCache\n{\npublic:\n    explicit LRUCache(std::size_t capacity)\n        : m_capacity(capacity)\n    {\n        if (capacity == 0)\n            throw std::invalid_argument(\"LRUCache capacity must be > 0\");\n    }\n\n    std::optional<Value> get(const Key& key)\n    {\n        std::unique_lock lock(m_mutex);\n        auto it = m_map.find(key);\n        if (it == m_map.end()) return std::nullopt;\n\n        // Move accessed element to front (most-recent)\n        m_list.splice(m_list.begin(), m_list, it->second);\n        return it->second->second;\n    }\n\n    void put(const Key& key, const Value& value)\n    {\n        std::unique_lock lock(m_mutex);\n\n        auto it = m_map.find(key);\n        if (it != m_map.end())\n        {\n            // Override existing entry\n            it->second->second = value;\n            m_list.splice(m_list.begin(), m_list, it->second);\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Insert new entry\n        m_list.emplace_front(key, value);\n        m_map[key] = m_list.begin();\n\n        // Evict if needed\n        if (m_map.size() > m_capacity)\n        {\n            auto last = m_list.end();\n            --last;\n            m_map.erase(last->first);\n            m_list.pop_back();\n        }\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    using ListType = std::list<std::pair<Key, Value>>;\n\n    std::size_t                         m_capacity;\n    ListType                            m_list;\n    std::unordered_map<Key,\n                       typename ListType::iterator,\n                       Hasher>          m_map;\n    mutable std::shared_mutex           m_mutex;\n};\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Voter Interfaces\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\nclass IAccessVoter\n{\npublic:\n    virtual ~IAccessVoter() = default;\n\n    /*\n     * Return true if this voter grants permission for the action on\n     * the resource by the given user. A voter that is not applicable\n     * should return std::nullopt.\n     */\n    virtual std::optional<bool>\n    vote(const UserContext&       user,\n         const ResourceDescriptor res,\n         std::string_view         action) const = 0;\n\nprotected:\n    // helper for inheritors\n    static bool roleIn(const UserContext& user, Role r)\n    {\n        return user.hasRole(r);\n    }\n};\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Concrete Voters\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n// 1. Role-based voter --------------------------------------------------------\nclass RoleVoter final : public IAccessVoter\n{\npublic:\n    std::optional<bool>\n    vote(const UserContext& user,\n         const ResourceDescriptor /*res*/,\n         std::string_view action) const override\n    {\n        if (action == \"admin\")\n        {\n            // Only admins may perform \"admin\" actions\n            return roleIn(user, Role::Admin) || roleIn(user, Role::SuperAdmin);\n        }\n\n        // Non-admin actions are not this voter's responsibility\n        return std::nullopt;\n    }\n};\n\n// 2. Ownership voter ---------------------------------------------------------\nclass OwnershipVoter final : public IAccessVoter\n{\npublic:\n    std::optional<bool>\n    vote(const UserContext& user,\n         const ResourceDescriptor res,\n         std::string_view action) const override\n    {\n        if (action == \"edit\" || action == \"delete\")\n        {\n            return res.ownerId == user.id || roleIn(user, Role::Editor) || roleIn(user, Role::SuperAdmin);\n        }\n\n        return std::nullopt;\n    }\n};\n\n// 3. Visibility / subscription voter ----------------------------------------\nclass VisibilityVoter final : public IAccessVoter\n{\npublic:\n    std::optional<bool>\n    vote(const UserContext& user,\n         const ResourceDescriptor res,\n         std::string_view action) const override\n    {\n        if (action != \"read\")\n            return std::nullopt;\n\n        if (res.isPublic) return true;\n        if (!user.authenticated) return false;\n\n        // Pretend a repository call that certifies premium subscription.\n        // We replace it with simple role check for demo purposes.\n        return res.isPremium ? roleIn(user, Role::Reader) || roleIn(user, Role::Author) ||\n                                   roleIn(user, Role::Editor) || roleIn(user, Role::Admin) ||\n                                   roleIn(user, Role::SuperAdmin)\n                             : true;\n    }\n};\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Permission Service (Affirmative-Based Decision Manager)\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\nclass PermissionService\n{\npublic:\n    // Dependency injection (repositories, config, etc.)\n    struct Dependencies\n    {\n        std::shared_ptr<IUserRepository>        userRepo;\n        std::shared_ptr<IArticleRepository>     articleRepo;\n        std::shared_ptr<ISubscriptionRepository> subscriptionRepo;\n    };\n\n    explicit PermissionService(Dependencies deps,\n                               std::size_t    cacheSize = 4'096)\n        : m_deps(std::move(deps))\n        , m_cache(cacheSize)\n    {\n        // Register built-in voters\n        m_voters.emplace_back(std::make_unique<RoleVoter>());\n        m_voters.emplace_back(std::make_unique<OwnershipVoter>());\n        m_voters.emplace_back(std::make_unique<VisibilityVoter>());\n    }\n\n    /*\n     * Evaluate permission for a user/action/resource triple.\n     * An \"affirmative\" strategy is used: the first voter that\n     * returns true grants access, while explicit false denies.\n     * If no voter returns a result, deny by default.\n     */\n    bool hasPermission(const UserContext& user,\n                       const ResourceDescriptor& resource,\n                       std::string_view action)\n    {\n        // Check cache\n        PermissionKey key{user.id, resource.ownerId /* acts as resourceId */, std::string(action)};\n        if (auto cached = m_cache.get(key))\n            return *cached;\n\n        bool result = evaluate(user, resource, action);\n\n        // Store in cache\n        m_cache.put(key, result);\n        return result;\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    bool evaluate(const UserContext& user,\n                  const ResourceDescriptor& resource,\n                  std::string_view action) const\n    {\n        // SuperAdmin shortcut\n        if (user.hasRole(Role::SuperAdmin))\n            return true;\n\n        // Delegating to voters\n        for (const auto& voter : m_voters)\n        {\n            try\n            {\n                std::optional<bool> voteResult = voter->vote(user, resource, action);\n\n                if (!voteResult.has_value())\n                    continue; // abstain \u2011> next voter\n\n                if (*voteResult)\n                    return true;  // grant immediately\n\n                // deny overrides all\n                return false;\n            }\n            catch (const std::exception& e)\n            {\n                // Defensive: log & move on to next voter\n                std::cerr << \"[security] Voter exception: \" << e.what() << '\\n';\n            }\n        }\n\n        // No voter granted access, deny by default\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    Dependencies                                     m_deps;\n    std::vector<std::unique_ptr<IAccessVoter>>       m_voters;\n    LRUCache<PermissionKey, bool, PermissionKeyHasher> m_cache;\n};\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Simple inline unit test (can be excluded in production builds)\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n#ifdef BLOGSUITE_SECURITY_SELFTEST\n#include <cassert>\n\nstatic void selfTest()\n{\n    PermissionService::Dependencies deps{/*nullptr, nullptr, nullptr*/};\n    PermissionService svc(deps, 32);\n\n    UserContext alice { \"alice\", {Role::Author}, true };\n    UserContext bob   { \"bob\",   {Role::Reader}, true };\n    UserContext admin { \"admin\", {Role::Admin},  true };\n\n    ResourceDescriptor pubArticle  { \"alice\", true,  false };\n    ResourceDescriptor privArticle { \"alice\", false, true  };\n\n    // Public read\n    assert( svc.hasPermission(bob, pubArticle, \"read\") );\n\n    // Private read w/o subscription -> deny\n    assert( !svc.hasPermission(bob, privArticle, \"read\") );\n\n    // Owner can edit\n    assert( svc.hasPermission(alice, pubArticle, \"edit\") );\n\n    // Non-owner cannot delete\n    assert( !svc.hasPermission(bob, pubArticle, \"delete\") );\n\n    // Admin can admin\n    assert( svc.hasPermission(admin, pubArticle, \"admin\") );\n\n    // Cache hit (repeat query)\n    assert( svc.hasPermission(admin, pubArticle, \"admin\") );\n}\n\nstatic int _ = (selfTest(), 0);\n#endif // BLOGSUITE_SECURITY_SELFTEST\n\n} // namespace intraledger::blogsuite::security\n```",

   // Executes a full-text search across available blog posts.\n    SearchResult search(std::string               query,\n                        core::auth::UserContext   user,\n This is the core security primitive used throughout the system.\n\n2. **Rate Limiting Layer** (module_33.cpp, module_46.cpp): Two complementary rate limiting mechanisms:\n   - `LoginAttemptThrottler`: Persistent, database-backed brute force protection with per-user and per-IP tracking\n   - `TokenBucketRateLimiter`: In-memory token bucket algorithm for general endpoint protection\n\n3. **Permission Layer** (module_39.cpp, module_52.cpp): RBAC implementation with two distinct patterns:\n   - `PermissionEvaluator`: Permission checking against role-based bitset permissions with caching\n   - `PermissionService`: Voter-based architecture (similar to Spring Security) with pluggable access control voters\n\n4. **Password Management** (module_56.cpp): Complete password reset workflow with secure token generation, rate limiting, and email dispatch integration\n\n### Dependency Key Interfaces Already Present\n\nThe codebase already demonstrates good interface design:\n\n1. **IUserRepository** - User data access abstraction\n2. **IUserRoleRepository** - Role membership queries\n3. **IPasswordResetRepository** - Token persistence\n4. **IEmailDispatcher** - Async email delivery\n5. **IAccessVoter** - Pluggable permission decision interface\n\n## Decoupling Strategy\n\n### Proposed Architecture: IAuthenticationService Interface\n\nTo extract the authentication system into a standalone SSO service, I propose introducing an abstract interface (`IAuthenticationService`) that follows the **Dependency Inversion Principle**. The main application would depend on this interface, not on concrete implementations.\n\n```cpp\nnamespace intraledger::auth {\n\n/**\n * Core authentication service interface.\n * This abstraction allows the BlogSuite to work with either:\n *   1. The embedded local implementation (current modules)\n *   2. A remote SSO service via HTTP/gRPC adapter\n */\nclass IAuthenticationService\n{\npublic:\n    virtual ~IAuthenticationService() = default;\n\n    // ===== Token Management =====\n\n    /**\n     * Generate an authentication token for a validated user.\n     * @param userId Unique user identifier\n     * @param roles User's assigned roles\n     * @param ttl Optional token lifetime\n     * @return Signed JWT-like token string\n     */\n    virtual std::string generateToken(\n        const std::string& userId,\n        const std::vector<std::string>& roles,\n        std::optional<std::chrono::seconds> ttl = std::nullopt) = 0;\n\n    /**\n     * Verify and decode a token.\n     * @param token The token string to validate\n     * @return Decoded claims on success\n     * @throws TokenExpired, TokenInvalid\n     */\n    virtual AuthClaims verifyToken(std::string_view token) = 0;\n\n    // ===== User Authentication =====\n\n    /**\n     * Authenticate user with credentials.\n     * @param email User email\n     * @param password Plain-text password\n     * @return AuthResult containing token and user info\n     * @throws AuthenticationFailed, AccountLocked\n     */\n    virtual AuthResult authenticate(\n        std::string_view email,\n        std::string_view password) = 0;\n\n    // ===== Password Management =====\n\n    /**\n     * Initiate password reset flow.\n     * @param email User's registered email\n     * @throws RateLimitExceeded\n     */\n    virtual void requestPasswordReset(std::string_view email) = 0;\n\n    /**\n     * Complete password reset with token.\n     * @param token Reset token from email\n     * @param newPassword New password (plain-text, will be hashed)\n     * @throws TokenInvalid, TokenExpired\n     */\n    virtual void resetPassword(\n        std::string_view token,\n        std::string_view newPassword) = 0;\n\n    // ===== Permission Checking =====\n\n    /**\n     * Check if user has permission for an action on a resource.\n     * @param userId User identifier\n     * @param action Action being performed (e.g., \"edit\", \"delete\")\n     * @param resourceId Target resource identifier\n     * @return true if permitted\n     */\n    virtual bool hasPermission(\n        const std::string& userId,\n        std::string_view action,\n        const std::string& resourceId) = 0;\n\n    // ===== Rate Limiting =====\n\n    /**\n     * Check if a login attempt is allowed (not rate limited).\n     * @param identifier IP address or user identifier\n     * @return true if attempt should proceed\n     */\n    virtual bool isLoginAttemptAllowed(const std::string& identifier) = 0;\n\n    /**\n     * Record a failed authentication attempt.\n     */\n    virtual void recordLoginFailure(\n        const std::optional<std::string>& userId,\n        const std::string& ipAddress) = 0;\n\n    /**\n     * Record a successful authentication (clears rate limits).\n     */\n    virtual void recordLoginSuccess(\n        const std::string& userId,\n        const std::string& ipAddress) = 0;\n};\n\n// Supporting data structures\nstruct AuthClaims\n{\n    std::string userId;\n    std::vector<std::string> roles;\n    std::chrono::system_clock::time_point issuedAt;\n    std::chrono::system_clock::time_point expiresAt;\n    std::string tokenId;  // jti\n};\n\nstruct AuthResult\n{\n    std::string token;\n    AuthClaims claims;\n    std::string refreshToken;  // Optional for token refresh flow\n};\n\n} // namespace intraledger::auth\n```\n\n### Implementation Strategy\n\n#### Phase 1: Create Interface and Local Implementation\n\n1. Define `IAuthenticationService` interface in a shared header\n2. Create `LocalAuthenticationService` that aggregates existing modules:\n   - Wraps `SecureTokenService` (module_74)\n   - Wraps `PasswordResetService` (module_56)\n   - Wraps `LoginAttemptThrottler` (module_33)\n   - Wraps `PermissionEvaluator` (module_39)\n   - Wraps `PermissionService` (module_52)\n\n```cpp\nclass LocalAuthenticationService : public IAuthenticationService\n{\npublic:\n    LocalAuthenticationService(\n        std::shared_ptr<SecureTokenService> tokenService,\n        std::shared_ptr<PasswordResetService> passwordService,\n        std::shared_ptr<LoginAttemptThrottler> throttler,\n        std::shared_ptr<PermissionEvaluator> permissions)\n        : m_tokenService(std::move(tokenService))\n        , m_passwordService(std::move(passwordService))\n        , m_throttler(std::move(throttler))\n        , m_permissions(std::move(permissions))\n    {}\n\n    // Implement interface methods by delegating to wrapped services\n    std::string generateToken(...) override { return m_tokenService->generateToken(...); }\n    AuthClaims verifyToken(...) override { return m_tokenService->verifyToken(...); }\n    // ...\n};\n```\n\n#### Phase 2: Create Remote SSO Adapter\n\nFor future SSO integration, implement a remote adapter:\n\n```cpp\nclass RemoteSSOAdapter : public IAuthenticationService\n{\npublic:\n    RemoteSSOAdapter(\n        std::string ssoBaseUrl,\n        std::string clientId,\n        std::string clientSecret,\n        std::shared_ptr<IHttpClient> httpClient)\n        : m_ssoUrl(std::move(ssoBaseUrl))\n        , m_clientId(std::move(clientId))\n        , m_clientSecret(std::move(clientSecret))\n        , m_http(std::move(httpClient))\n    {}\n\n    std::string generateToken(...) override\n    {\n        // POST /api/v1/tokens to SSO service\n        auto response = m_http->post(m_ssoUrl + \"/api/v1/tokens\", payload);\n        return response.json()[\"token\"];\n    }\n\n    AuthClaims verifyToken(std::string_view token) override\n    {\n        // POST /api/v1/tokens/verify or use local JWT validation\n        // with SSO public key\n    }\n    // ...\n};\n```\n\n#### Phase 3: Update Dependent Modules\n\nModify consumers to use the interface via dependency injection:\n\n```cpp\n// Before (tightly coupled)\nclass PostSearchService\n{\n    std::shared_ptr<PermissionEvaluator> m_permissions;\n};\n\n// After (loosely coupled)\nclass PostSearchService\n{\n    std::shared_ptr<IAuthenticationService> m_auth;\n\n    // Use:\n    if (m_auth->hasPermission(userId, \"read\", articleId)) { ... }\n};\n```\n\n### Benefits of This Approach\n\n1. **Minimal Code Changes**: Existing modules remain intact; we wrap rather than rewrite\n2. **Gradual Migration**: Switch from `LocalAuthenticationService` to `RemoteSSOAdapter` per-service\n3. **Testability**: Easy to mock `IAuthenticationService` for unit tests\n4. **Separation of Concerns**: Clear boundary between auth logic and business logic\n5. **Configuration-Driven**: Swap implementations via DI container configuration\n\n### API Contract for Future SSO Service\n\n```yaml\n# OpenAPI 3.0 specification snippet\npaths:\n  /api/v1/auth/login:\n    post:\n      summary: Authenticate user\n      requestBody:\n        content:\n          application/json:\n            schema:\n              type: object\n              properties:\n                email: { type: string }\n                password: { type: string }\n      responses:\n        200:\n          description: Authentication successful\n          content:\n            application/json:\n              schema:\n                $ref: '#/components/schemas/AuthResult'\n\n  /api/v1/auth/tokens/verify:\n    post:\n      summary: Verify token validity\n      requestBody:\n        content:\n          application/json:\n            schema:\n              type: object\n              properties:\n                token: { type: string }\n\n  /api/v1/auth/password-reset/request:\n    post:\n      summary: Request password reset\n\n  /api/v1/auth/password-reset/complete:\n    post:\n      summary: Complete password reset with token\n\n  /api/v1/auth/permissions/check:\n    post:\n      summary: Check user permission\n```\n\n## Summary\n\n- **Primary finding**: The authentication system is distributed across six core modules implementing token management, password reset, rate limiting, and RBAC/permission checking. The codebase already exhibits good interface design with abstract base classes.\n\n- **Key components**:\n  - **module_74.cpp**: SecureTokenService (JWT-like token generation/validation)\n  - **module_56.cpp**: PasswordResetService (password reset workflow)\n  - **module_33.cpp**: LoginAttemptThrottler (brute force protection)\n  - **module_39.cpp**: PermissionEvaluator (RBAC with caching)\n  - **module_52.cpp**: PermissionService (voter-based access control)\n  - **module_46.cpp**: TokenBucketRateLimiter (rate limiting middleware)\n\n- **Dependent modules**: module_24, module_51, module_64, module_66 consume authentication services for RBAC filtering, notifications, and user context management.\n\n- **Architectural pattern**: The recommended decoupling strategy is to introduce an `IAuthenticationService` abstract interface following the **Dependency Inversion Principle**. This allows the BlogSuite to depend on the interface rather than concrete implementations, enabling seamless swapping between a local implementation (wrapping existing modules) and a remote SSO adapter for the future centralized authentication service.\n\n- **Recommendations**:\n  1. Create the `IAuthenticationService` interface with methods for token management, authentication, password reset, and permission checking\n  2. Implement `LocalAuthenticationService` as a facade over existing modules\n  3. Update dependent modules to use the interface via dependency injection\n  4. Later implement `RemoteSSOAdapter` that communicates with the external SSO service via HTTP/gRPC\n  5. Use configuration-driven factory to swap implementations without code changes\n",

This is the core security primitive used throughout the system.\n\n2. **Rate Limiting Layer** (module_33.cpp, module_46.cpp): Two complementary rate limiting mechanisms:\n   - `LoginAttemptThrottler`: Persistent, database-backed brute force protection with per-user and per-IP tracking\n   - `TokenBucketRateLimiter`: In-memory token bucket algorithm for general endpoint protection\n\n3. **Permission Layer** (module_39.cpp, module_52.cpp): RBAC implementation with two distinct patterns:\n   - `PermissionEvaluator`: Permission checking against role-based bitset permissions with caching\n   - `PermissionService`: Voter-based architecture (similar to Spring Security) with pluggable access control voters\n\n4. **Password Management** (module_56.cpp): Complete password reset workflow with secure token generation, rate limiting, and email dispatch integration\n\n### Dependency Key Interfaces Already Present\n\nThe codebase already demonstrates good interface design:\n\n1. **IUserRepository** - User data access abstraction\n2. **IUserRoleRepository** - Role membership queries\n3. **IPasswordResetRepository** - Token persistence\n4. **IEmailDispatcher** - Async email delivery\n5. **IAccessVoter** - Pluggable permission decision interface\n\n## Decoupling Strategy\n\n### Proposed Architecture: IAuthenticationService Interface\n\nTo extract the authentication system into a standalone SSO service, I propose introducing an abstract interface (`IAuthenticationService`) that follows the **Dependency Inversion Principle**. The main application would depend on this interface, not on concrete implementations.\n\n```cpp\nnamespace intraledger::auth {\n\n/**\n * Core authentication service interface.\n * This abstraction allows the BlogSuite to work with either:\n *   1. The embedded local implementation (current modules)\n *   2. A remote SSO service via HTTP/gRPC adapter\n */\nclass IAuthenticationService\n{\npublic:\n    virtual ~IAuthenticationService() = default;\n\n    // ===== Token Management =====\n\n    /**\n     * Generate an authentication token for a validated user.\n     * @param userId Unique user identifier\n     * @param roles User's assigned roles\n     * @param ttl Optional token lifetime\n     * @return Signed JWT-like token string\n     */\n    virtual std::string generateToken(\n        const std::string& userId,\n        const std::vector<std::string>& roles,\n        std::optional<std::chrono::seconds> ttl = std::nullopt) = 0;\n\n    /**\n     * Verify and decode a token.\n     * @param token The token string to validate\n     * @return Decoded claims on success\n     * @throws TokenExpired, TokenInvalid\n     */\n    virtual AuthClaims verifyToken(std::string_view token) = 0;\n\n    // ===== User Authentication =====\n\n    /**\n     * Authenticate user with credentials.\n     * @param email User email\n     * @param password Plain-text password\n     * @return AuthResult containing token and user info\n     * @throws AuthenticationFailed, AccountLocked\n     */\n    virtual AuthResult authenticate(\n        std::string_view email,\n        std::string_view password) = 0;\n\n    // ===== Password Management =====\n\n    /**\n     * Initiate password reset flow.\n     * @param email User's registered email\n     * @throws RateLimitExceeded\n     */\n    virtual void requestPasswordReset(std::string_view email) = 0;\n\n    /**\n     * Complete password reset with token.\n     * @param token Reset token from email\n     * @param newPassword New password (plain-text, will be hashed)\n     * @throws TokenInvalid, TokenExpired\n     */\n    virtual void resetPassword(\n        std::string_view token,\n        std::string_view newPassword) = 0;\n\n    // ===== Permission Checking =====\n\n    /**\n     * Check if user has permission for an action on a resource.\n     * @param userId User identifier\n     * @param action Action being performed (e.g., \"edit\", \"delete\")\n     * @param resourceId Target resource identifier\n     * @return true if permitted\n     */\n    virtual bool hasPermission(\n        const std::string& userId,\n        std::string_view action,\n        const std::string& resourceId) = 0;\n\n    // ===== Rate Limiting =====\n\n    /**\n     * Check if a login attempt is allowed (not rate limited).\n     * @param identifier IP address or user identifier\n     * @return true if attempt should proceed\n     */\n    virtual bool isLoginAttemptAllowed(const std::string& identifier) = 0;\n\n    /**\n     * Record a failed authentication attempt.\n     */\n    virtual void recordLoginFailure(\n        const std::optional<std::string>& userId,\n        const std::string& ipAddress) = 0;\n\n    /**\n     * Record a successful authentication (clears rate limits).\n     */\n    virtual void recordLoginSuccess(\n        const std::string& userId,\n        const std::string& ipAddress) = 0;\n};\n\n// Supporting data structures\nstruct AuthClaims\n{\n    std::string userId;\n    std::vector<std::string> roles;\n    std::chrono::system_clock::time_point issuedAt;\n    std::chrono::system_clock::time_point expiresAt;\n    std::string tokenId;  // jti\n};\n\nstruct AuthResult\n{\n    std::string token;\n    AuthClaims claims;\n    std::string refreshToken;  // Optional for token refresh flow\n};\n\n} // namespace intraledger::auth\n```\n\n### Implementation Strategy\n\n#### Phase 1: Create Interface and Local Implementation\n\n1. Define `IAuthenticationService` interface in a shared header\n2. Create `LocalAuthenticationService` that aggregates existing modules:\n   - Wraps `SecureTokenService` (module_74)\n   - Wraps `PasswordResetService` (module_56)\n   - Wraps `LoginAttemptThrottler` (module_33)\n   - Wraps `PermissionEvaluator` (module_39)\n   - Wraps `PermissionService` (module_52)\n\n```cpp\nclass LocalAuthenticationService : public IAuthenticationService\n{\npublic:\n    LocalAuthenticationService(\n        std::shared_ptr<SecureTokenService> tokenService,\n        std::shared_ptr<PasswordResetService> passwordService,\n        std::shared_ptr<LoginAttemptThrottler> throttler,\n        std::shared_ptr<PermissionEvaluator> permissions)\n        : m_tokenService(std::move(tokenService))\n        , m_passwordService(std::move(passwordService))\n        , m_throttler(std::move(throttler))\n        , m_permissions(std::move(permissions))\n    {}\n\n    // Implement interface methods by delegating to wrapped services\n    std::string generateToken(...) override { return m_tokenService->generateToken(...); }\n    AuthClaims verifyToken(...) override { return m_tokenService->verifyToken(...); }\n    // ...\n};\n```\n\n#### Phase 2: Create Remote SSO Adapter\n\nFor future SSO integration, implement a remote adapter:\n\n```cpp\nclass RemoteSSOAdapter : public IAuthenticationService\n{\npublic:\n    RemoteSSOAdapter(\n        std::string ssoBaseUrl,\n        std::string clientId,\n        std::string clientSecret,\n        std::shared_ptr<IHttpClient> httpClient)\n        : m_ssoUrl(std::move(ssoBaseUrl))\n        , m_clientId(std::move(clientId))\n        , m_clientSecret(std::move(clientSecret))\n        , m_http(std::move(httpClient))\n    {}\n\n    std::string generateToken(...) override\n    {\n        // POST /api/v1/tokens to SSO service\n        auto response = m_http->post(m_ssoUrl + \"/api/v1/tokens\", payload);\n        return response.json()[\"token\"];\n    }\n\n    AuthClaims verifyToken(std::string_view token) override\n    {\n        // POST /api/v1/tokens/verify or use local JWT validation\n        // with SSO public key\n    }\n    // ...\n};\n```\n\n#### Phase 3: Update Dependent Modules\n\nModify consumers to use the interface via dependency injection:\n\n```cpp\n// Before (tightly coupled)\nclass PostSearchService\n{\n    std::shared_ptr<PermissionEvaluator> m_permissions;\n};\n\n// After (loosely coupled)\nclass PostSearchService\n{\n    std::shared_ptr<IAuthenticationService> m_auth;\n\n    // Use:\n    if (m_auth->hasPermission(userId, \"read\", articleId)) { ... }\n};\n```\n\n### Benefits of This Approach\n\n1. **Minimal Code Changes**: Existing modules remain intact; we wrap rather than rewrite\n2. **Gradual Migration**: Switch from `LocalAuthenticationService` to `RemoteSSOAdapter` per-service\n3. **Testability**: Easy to mock `IAuthenticationService` for unit tests\n4. **Separation of Concerns**: Clear boundary between auth logic and business logic\n5. **Configuration-Driven**: Swap implementations via DI container configuration\n\n### API Contract for Future SSO Service\n\n```yaml\n# OpenAPI 3.0 specification snippet\npaths:\n  /api/v1/auth/login:\n    post:\n      summary: Authenticate user\n      requestBody:\n        content:\n          application/json:\n            schema:\n              type: object\n              properties:\n                email: { type: string }\n                password: { type: string }\n      responses:\n        200:\n          description: Authentication successful\n          content:\n            application/json:\n              schema:\n                $ref: '#/components/schemas/AuthResult'\n\n  /api/v1/auth/tokens/verify:\n    post:\n      summary: Verify token validity\n      requestBody:\n        content:\n          application/json:\n            schema:\n              type: object\n              properties:\n                token: { type: string }\n\n  /api/v1/auth/password-reset/request:\n    post:\n      summary: Request password reset\n\n  /api/v1/auth/password-reset/complete:\n    post:\n      summary: Complete password reset with token\n\n  /api/v1/auth/permissions/check:\n    post:\n      summary: Check user permission\n```\n\n## Summary\n\n- **Primary finding**: The authentication system is distributed across six core modules implementing token management, password reset, rate limiting, and RBAC/permission checking. The codebase already exhibits good interface design with abstract base classes.\n\n- **Key components**:\n  - **module_74.cpp**: SecureTokenService (JWT-like token generation/validation)\n  - **module_56.cpp**: PasswordResetService (password reset workflow)\n  - **module_33.cpp**: LoginAttemptThrottler (brute force protection)\n  - **module_39.cpp**: PermissionEvaluator (RBAC with caching)\n  - **module_52.cpp**: PermissionService (voter-based access control)\n  - **module_46.cpp**: TokenBucketRateLimiter (rate limiting middleware)\n\n- **Dependent modules**: module_24, module_51, module_64, module_66 consume authentication services for RBAC filtering, notifications, and user context management.\n\n- **Architectural pattern**: The recommended decoupling strategy is to introduce an `IAuthenticationService` abstract interface following the **Dependency Inversion Principle**. This allows the BlogSuite to depend on the interface rather than concrete implementations, enabling seamless swapping between a local implementation (wrapping existing modules) and a remote SSO adapter for the future centralized authentication service.\n\n- **Recommendations**:\n  1. Create the `IAuthenticationService` interface with methods for token management, authentication, password reset, and permission checking\n  2. Implement `LocalAuthenticationService` as a facade over existing modules\n  3. Update dependent modules to use the interface via dependency injection\n  4. Later implement `RemoteSSOAdapter` that communicates with the external SSO service via HTTP/gRPC\n  5. Use configuration-driven factory to swap implementations without code changes\n",

# Solution: cpp_web_blog_expert_040_architectural_understanding_expert_01

## Key Files Identified

### Core Authentication/Security Modules

- **/app/project/src/module_74.cpp** - SecureTokenService: JWT-like token generation/validation using HMAC-SHA256 signing, base64url encoding, expiration handling
- **/app/project/src/module_56.cpp** - PasswordResetService: Secure password reset workflow with rate-limiting, token generation, email dispatch integration
- **/app/project/src/module_33.cpp** - LoginAttemptThrottler: Brute-force protection, per-user and per-IP rate limiting, DB-persisted counters
- **/app/project/src/module_39.cpp** - RBAC PermissionEvaluator: Role-based access control, permission caching with TTL, user role evaluation
- **/app/project/src/module_52.cpp** - PermissionService: Voter-based access control system, LRU decision cache, role/ownership/visibility voters
- **/app/project/src/module_46.cpp** - TokenBucketRateLimiter: Token-bucket based rate limiting middleware for login and other endpoints

### Dependent/Consumer Modules

- **/app/project/src/module_51.cpp** - EmailNotificationService: Uses auth for password reset emails (Notification::Type::PasswordReset)
- **/app/project/src/module_24.cpp** - PostSearchService: Imports core/auth/UserContext.hpp for RBAC-aware search filtering
- **/app/project/src/module_64.cpp** - SearchService: Imports middleware/UserContext.hpp for role-based result filtering
- **/app/project/src/module_66.cpp** - ContentMetricsService: Uses UserContext for view deduplication based on authenticated user

### Supporting Infrastructure

- **/app/project/src/constants.cpp** - Application constants including kHeaderAuthorization, kEnvSecretKey
- **/app/project/tests/test_main.cpp** - Test suite referencing blog::auth::PasswordHa
